--CREATE SEQUENCES

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_ESTADO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_CIDADE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_BAIRRO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;


CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_LOGRADOURO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_ENDERECO_PACIENTE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_TIPO_CONTATO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHTSTU_UNID_HOSPITALAR
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_MEDICO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_MEDICAMENTO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_PRESCRICAO_MEDICA
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_PACIENTE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_EMAIL_PACIENTE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_PLANO_SAUDE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_PACIENTE_PLANO_SAUDE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_FORMA_PAGAMENTO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;

CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_CONSULTA_FORMA_PAGTO
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;
 
CREATE SEQUENCE SQ_RHSTU_TELEFONE_PACIENTE
    START WITH 1 
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NOCACHE;   
        
-- DROP SEQUENCES
